)@@G@@         SUBROUTINE COPY (N)  @@@[@@@M@[@@ 00161*             1         RP
)@@G@@  SUBROUTINE COPY (N)                                               COP0RQ
)@@G@@0010  @M@[@@ 00162*                   C                                 RR
)@@G@@                                      COP00020  @M@[@@ 00163*           RS
)@@G@@        C     THIS SUBROUTINE COPYS NON-BLANK CHARACTERS FROM JINT TO IORT
)@@G@@UT.     COP00030  @M@[@@ 00164*                   C                     RU
)@@G@@                                                  COP00040  @M@[@@ 00165RV
)@@G@@*                   C                        ===   ON ENTRY   ===       RW
)@@G@@                    COP00050  @M@[@@ 00166*                   C     N .LRX
)@@G@@T. 0 COPYS UNTIL PARENTHESIS COUNT IS ZERO.                   COP00060  RY
)@@G@@@M@[@@ 00167*                   C     N .EQ. 0 COPYS ALL REMAINING NON-BRZ
)@@G@@LANK DATA FROM JINT TO IOUT.    COP00070  @M@[@@ 00168*                 SA
)@@G@@  C     N .GT. 0 COPYS N NON-BLANK DATA FROM JINT TO IOUT.              SB
)@@G@@  COP00080  @M@[@@ 00169*                   C     THE FIRST ITEM INSPECTSC
)@@G@@ED IS JINT(JCOL).                           COP00090  @M@[@@ 00170*     SD
)@@G@@              C     THE FIRST ITEM STORED GOES TO IOUT(ICOL+1).         SE
)@@G@@              COP00100  @M@[@@ 00171*                   C               SF
)@@G@@                                                        COP00110  @M@[@@SG
)@@G@@ 00172*                   C                        ===   ON EXIT   ===  SH
)@@G@@                          COP00120  @M@[@@ 00173*                   C   SI
)@@G@@  MEOF .LT. 0  FOR NORMAL EXIT.                                     COP0SJ
)@@G@@0130  @M@[@@ 00174*                   C     MEOF .EQ. 0  FOR KERM FOUND SK
)@@G@@WHILE COPYING  ALL REMAINING DATA,    COP00140  @M@[@@ 00175*           SL
)@@G@@        C                  OR FOR KERM FOUND BEFORE LEFT PARENTHESIS.   SM
)@@G@@        COP00150  @M@[@@ 00176*                   C     MEOF .GT. 0  FORSN
)@@G@@ MISSING RIGHT PARENTHESIS, OR FOR MEOF =0 ON     COP00160  @M@[@@ 00177SO
)@@G@@*                   C                  ENTRY TO COPY.                   SP
)@@G@@                    COP00170  @M@[@@ 00178*                   C         SQ
)@@G@@                                                              COP00180  SR
)@@G@@@M@[@@ 00179*                   C     THE LAST ITEM STORED WENT TO IOUT(SS
)@@G@@ICOL) AND IS IN LCPY.           COP00190  @M@[@@ 00180*                 ST
)@@G@@  C     IF MEOF IS .LT. 0, THE NEXT NON-BLANK ITEM IS IN JINT(JCOL) AND SU
)@@G@@  COP00200  @M@[@@ 00181*                   C     IN PNEXT.             SV
)@@G@@                                            COP00210  @M@[@@ 00182*     SW
)@@G@@              C                                                         SX
